 Who was Haji Mastanhaji Mastan Mirza was born on 1 March 1926 in Cuddalore, Tamil Nadu
 uske pita haidar mirza ek garib kisaan the
 His family was financially weak
 kai baar ghar main khaane ke liye bhi paise nahin hote the

 tab haidar mirza ne aakhirkaar baahar jaakar paisa kamaane kaa man banaaya

 vahaan unhone kai kaam kiye magar kamyaabi nahin mili

 1996 ke aam chunaav main pi
 V
